\newcommand\lthtmllogmath{\dimen0\ht\sizebox \advance\dimen0\dp\sizebox
  \ifdim\dimen0>.95\vsize
   \lthtmltypeout{%
*** image for \lthtmlmathenv\space is too tall at \the\dimen0, reducing to .95 vsize ***}%
   \ht\sizebox.95\vsize \dp\sizebox\z@ \fi
  \lthtmltypeout{l2hSize %
:\lthtmlmathenv:\the\ht\sizebox::\the\dp\sizebox::\the\wd\sizebox.\preveqno}}%

       \lthtmlmathtype{#1}\lthtmlvboxmathA}%

  \vrule height1.5ex width0pt }%

\def\lthtmlsetinline{\hbox{\vrule width.1em \vtop{\vbox{%
  \kern.1em\copy\sizebox}\ifdim\dp\sizebox>0pt\kern.1em\else\kern.3pt\fi
  \ifdim\hsize>\wd\sizebox \hrule depth1pt\fi}}}
\def\lthtmlsetmath{\hbox{\vrule width.1em\kern-.05em\vtop{\vbox{%
  \kern.1em\kern0.8 pt\hbox{\hglue.17em\copy\sizebox\hglue0.8 pt}}\kern.3pt%
  \ifdim\dp\sizebox>0pt\kern.1em\fi \kern0.8 pt%
  \ifdim\hsize>\wd\sizebox \hrule depth1pt\fi}}}
\def\centerinlinemath{%
  \dimen1=\ifdim\ht\sizebox<\dp\sizebox \dp\sizebox\else\ht\sizebox\fi
  \advance\dimen1by.5pt \vrule width0pt height\dimen1 depth\dimen1 
 \dp\sizebox=\dimen1\ht\sizebox=\dimen1\relax}

\stepcounter{subsection}
\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm515}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 515
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Depth-First zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueFront}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm551}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 551
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Breadth-First zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueBack}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%

\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm587}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 587
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Non-Deterministic zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueRandom}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm621}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 621
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Iterative Deepening zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\STATE $\mbox{depth}\leftarrow1$\COMMENT{Or any other offset depth}
\WHILE{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Start Depth-Limited Search}
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf depth}\left( r \right)}<\mbox{depth}$}
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueFront}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\STATE\COMMENT{End Depth-Limited Search}
\STATE $\mbox{depth}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}+1$
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm664}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 664
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Bi-Directional zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}_1\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}_2\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the goal}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue}_1 \right)}\wedge\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue}_2 \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf shareState}\left( \mbox{Queue}_1,\mbox{Queue}_2 \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue}_1 \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueBack}\left( \mbox{Queue}_1,R \right)}$
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue}_2 \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewReversedPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueBack}\left( \mbox{Queue}_2,R \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf shareState}\left( \mbox{Queue}_1,\mbox{Queue}_2 \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm708}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 708
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Hill Climbing zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf quickSort}\left( R,h\left(R_i\right) \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueFront}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}

\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23330}%
$ w$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23332}%

\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm736}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 736
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Beam Search zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{nextdepth}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{nextdepth} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{nextdepth}$
\STATE $\mbox{nextdepth}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\mbox{nextdepth}\leftarrow\mbox{nextdepth}\cup R$
\WHILE{$\#\mbox{nextdepth}>w$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Verwijder pad met de hoogste heuristiek uit $\mbox{nextdepth}$}
\STATE $\mbox{nextdepth}\leftarrow\mbox{nextdepth}\setminus\left\{\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf max}_{h}\left( R \right)}\right\}$
\ENDWHILE
\ENDWHILE
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\caption{Hill Climbing 2 zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $r\leftarrow\mbox{root}$
\WHILE{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( r \right)}$}
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( R \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf max}_{h}\left( R \right)}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%

\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueue}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$\COMMENT{De plaats doet er niet toe, de $\mbox{Queue}$\  wordt nog gesorteerd}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm960}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 960
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Path Deletion Principe}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\IF{$P\in\mbox{Queue}\wedge P=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I\right)\wedge Q\in\mbox{Queue}\wedge Q=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I,\ldots\right)\wedge c\left(P\right)\geq c\left(Q\right)$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf delete}\left( \mbox{Queue},P \right)}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm972}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 972
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{A* zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue}\left[0\right] \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueue}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$\COMMENT{De plaats doet er niet toe, de $\mbox{Queue}$\  wordt nog gesorteerd}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf quickSort}\left( \mbox{Queue},f \right)}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Path Deletion}
\FORALL{$P,Q\in\mbox{Queue}$}
\IF{$P=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I\right)\wedge Q=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I,\ldots\right)\wedge c\left(P\right)\geq c\left(Q\right)$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf delete}\left( \mbox{Queue},P \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue}\left[0\right] \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{success}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23473}%
$ \qedsymbol$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23486}%
$ \begin{array}{ll}
\mbox{\underline{Initieel:} }&S=\mbox{pad die de bron bevat } \in\mbox{Queue}\wedge S \mbox{ is een subpad van } B\\
&\Downarrow\\
&\mbox{subpad van }B\in\mbox{Queue}\\\\
\mbox{\underline{Iteratie:} }&\mbox{indien een subpad van $B$\  verwijdert wordt}\\\\
&\mbox{- het subpad heeft ten minste een kind (anders bestaat er geen $B$)}\\
&\mbox{- bovendien bevat dat kind geen lus ($B$\  bevat geen lus)}\\\\
&\Rightarrow\mbox{Dit kind wordt weer toegevoegd aan de $\mbox{Queue}$}\\
&\Rightarrow\mbox{een subpad van }B\in\mbox{Queue}\\\\
\end{array}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23495}%
$ f\left(p\right)>c\left(B\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23502}%
$ \begin{array}{rcl}
\mbox{altijd een subpad $q$\  van}&\wedge&f\left(q\right)\leq c\left(B\right)<f\left(p\right)\\
\mbox{$B$\  met } f\left(q\right)\leq c\left(B\right)&&\\
&\Downarrow&\\
\multicolumn{3}{c}{\mbox{$p$\  wordt nooit geselecteerd}}
\end{array}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm1087}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 1087
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Geoptimaliseerd Path Deletion Principe}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE ${\mathfrak{H}}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\IF{A* selecteerd een pad $p$}
\STATE $s\leftarrow p_{\mbox{end state}}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hashtableContains}\left( {\mathfrak{H}},s \right)}$}
\STATE do not evaluate $p$
\ELSE
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf insertHashtable}\left( {\mathfrak{H}},s \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

$ f\left(S,\ldots,A,B\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23626}%
$ f\left(S,\ldots,A\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23630}%
$ f'$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay23632}%
$\displaystyle f'\left(S,\ldots,A,B\right)=\ensuremath{\mbox{max}\left( c\left(S,\ldots,A,B\right)+h\left(B\right),f'\left(S,\ldots,A\right) \right)}$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23651}%
$ f\left(S\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm1112}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 1112
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Iterative Deepening A* zoekalgoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{$f$-bound}\leftarrow f\left(S\right)$\COMMENT{Or another $\mbox{$f$-bound}$-offset value}
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\WHILE{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf goalReached}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Begin $f$-limited Search}
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\mbox{Path containing the root}$
\STATE $\mbox{$f$-new}\leftarrow\infty$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE $r\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE $R\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf createNewPaths}\left( r \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeLoops}\left( R \right)}$
\STATE $\mbox{$f$-new}\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf min}_{}\left( \mbox{$f$-new},f\left(\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf min}_{f}\left( \ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( R,\left(R_i\right)>\mbox{$f$-bound} \right)} \right)}\right) \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeIf}\left( R,f\left(R_i\right)>\mbox{$f$-bound} \right)}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Because we will evaluate them all the nodes lower than}
\STATE\COMMENT{a certain $f$-value we don't have to sort them in any order}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueueFront}\left( \mbox{Queue},R \right)}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Path Deletion}
\IF{$P,Q\in\mbox{Queue}\wedge P=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I\right)\wedge Q=\left(\mbox{root},\ldots,I,\ldots\right)\wedge c\left(P\right)\geq c\left(Q\right)$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf delete}\left( \mbox{Queue},P \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\STATE\COMMENT{Einde $f$-limited Search}
\STATE $\mbox{$f$-bound}\leftarrow\mbox{$f$-new}$
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23659}%
$ \mathcal{O}\left(N^2\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline23661}%
$ \mathcal{O}\left(b\cdot c\left(B\right)/\delta\right)$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{subsection}
\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage

$\displaystyle f\left(p\right)=\left.\omega\cdot c\left(p\right)+h\left(p_{\mbox{end state}}\right)\  \ \  \ \right|\omega\in\left[0,1\right]$%

\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm6997}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 6997
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Find-S}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $h\leftarrow\perp$
\FORALL{$d\in D\wedge c\left(d\right)$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE $h\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimalGeneralisationThatCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\caption{Dual Find-S}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment

\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7062}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7062
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Grofstructuur van het Version-Spaces algoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE\COMMENT{Verzameling van hypotheses die vanuit de meest algemene hypothese vertrekken}
\STATE $G\leftarrow\left\{\left[\mbox{?},\mbox{?},\ldots,\mbox{?}\right]\right\}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Verzameling van hypotheses die vanuit de meest specifieke hypothese vertrekken}
\STATE $S\leftarrow\left\{\perp\right\}$
\FORALL{$d\in D$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( G \right)}\vee\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( S \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Dit treed op indien de testdata tegenstrijdige informatie bevat}
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\IF{$c\left(d\right)$}
\STATE\COMMENT{positieve test-situatie}
\FORALL{$h\in S$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Een hypothese heeft een probleem met de test-situatie}
\STATE\COMMENT{Oplossing}
\STATE $\ldots$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\STATE\COMMENT{Alle problemen zijn opgelost}
\ELSE
\STATE\COMMENT{negatieve test-situatie}
\FORALL{$h\in G$}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Een hypothese heeft een probleem met de test-situatie}
\STATE\COMMENT{Oplossing}
\STATE $\ldots$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\STATE\COMMENT{Alle problemen zijn opgelost}
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7101}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7101
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Complete implementatie van het Version-Spaces algoritme}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $G\leftarrow\left\{\left[\mbox{?},\mbox{?},\ldots,\mbox{?}\right]\right\}$
\STATE $S\leftarrow\left\{\perp\right\}$
\FORALL{$d\in D$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( G \right)}\vee\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( S \right)}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\IF{$c\left(d\right)$}
\FORALL{$h\in S$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE $S^+\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimalGeneralisationsThatCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeIf}\left( S^+,\forall g\in G:\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf isSpecialisationOf}\left( S^+[i],g \right)} \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeIf}\left( S^+,\exists s\in S\cup S^+:\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf isGeneralisationOf}\left( S^+[i],s \right)} \right)}$
\STATE $S\leftarrow S\cup S^+$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\FORALL{$h\in G$}
\IF{$\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE $G\leftarrow G\setminus\left\{h\right\}$\COMMENT{Pruning}
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\ELSE
\FORALL{$h\in G$}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE $G^+\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimalSpecialisationsThatNotCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeIf}\left( G^+,\forall s\in S:\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf isGeneralisationOf}\left( G^+[i],s \right)} \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeIf}\left( G^+,\exists g\in G\cup G^+:\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf isSpecialisationOf}\left( G^+[i],g \right)} \right)}$
\STATE $G\leftarrow G\cup G^+$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\FORALL{$h\in S$}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE $S\leftarrow S\setminus\left\{h\right\}$\COMMENT{Pruning}
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7137}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7137
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Conclusie trekken uit een Version-space}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE$n^+\leftarrow0$
\STATE$n^-\leftarrow0$
\FORALL{$h\in S\cup G$}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf hypothesisCovers}\left( h,d \right)}$}
\STATE$n^+\leftarrow n^++1$
\ELSE
\STATE$n^-\leftarrow n^-+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\IF{$n^-=0$}
\RETURN $\mbox{\bf true}$
\ELSIF{$n^+=0$}
\RETURN $\mbox{\bf false}$
\ELSIF{$n^+>n^-$}
\RETURN ``$\mbox{\bf true}$\  with a probability of $n^+/(n^++n^-)$''
\ELSIF{$n^+<n^-$}
\RETURN ``$\mbox{\bf false}$\  with a probability of $n^-/(n^++n^-)$''
\ELSE[$n^+=n^-$]
\RETURN ``no conclusion''
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7209}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7209
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf chronologicalBacktracking}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\FOR{$k=1$\  to $n_{\mbox{depth}}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Iteratie over alle knopen op niveau $\mbox{depth}$}
\STATE$z_{\mbox{depth}}\leftarrow a_{\mbox{depth}\,k}$\COMMENT{Geef $z_{\mbox{depth}}$\  een concrete waarde}
\STATE$b\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Controleer alle constraints met $z_i$}
\FOR{$j=1$\  to $\mbox{depth}-1$}
\STATE $b\leftarrow b\wedge c\left(z_j,z_i\right)$
\ENDFOR
\IF{$b$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Alle constraints kloppen}
\IF{$\mbox{depth}=n$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Laatste niveau bereikt, oplossing gevonden!}
\RETURN$\left(z_1,z_2,\ldots,z_n\right)$
\ELSE
\STATE\COMMENT{Naar het volgende niveau}
\STATE$\mbox{depth}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}+1$
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf chronologicalBacktracking}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$
\STATE$\mbox{depth}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}-1$
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7238}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7238
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf backjumping}\left( \mbox{depth},\mbox{\bf out: }l \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $l\leftarrow0$
\FOR{$k=1$\  to $n_{\mbox{depth}}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Iteratie over alle knopen op niveau $\mbox{depth}$}
\STATE$z_{\mbox{depth}}\leftarrow a_{\mbox{depth}\,k}$\COMMENT{Geef $z_{\mbox{depth}}$\  een concrete waarde}
\STATE$b\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$
\STATE\COMMENT{Controleer alle constraints met $z_i$}
\FOR{$j=1$\  to $\mbox{depth}-1$}
\IF{$b\wedge\neg c\left(z_j,z_i\right)$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Eerst falende conditie}
\STATE $b\leftarrow\mbox{\bf false}$
\STATE $l\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf max}_{}\left( l,j \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\IF{$b$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Alle constraints kloppen}
\IF{$\mbox{depth}=n$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Laatste niveau bereikt, oplossing gevonden!}
\RETURN$\left(z_1,z_2,\ldots,z_n\right)$
\ELSE
\STATE\COMMENT{Naar het volgende niveau}
\STATE$\mbox{depth}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}+1$
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf backjumping}\left( \mbox{depth},\mbox{\bf out: }L \right)}$
\STATE$\mbox{depth}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}-1$
\IF{$L<\mbox{depth}$}
\RETURN
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage

$ \ensuremath{\mbox{Backup}\left( k \right)}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24155}%
$ \ensuremath{\mbox{Checkdepth}\left( k,l \right)}<\ensuremath{\mbox{Backup}\left( k \right)}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7290}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7290
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf backmarking}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\FOR{$k=1$\  to $n_{\mbox{depth}}$}
\STATE $z_{\mbox{depth}}\leftarrow a_{\mbox{depth}\,k}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf Checkdepth}\left( \mbox{depth},k \right)}\geq\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf Backup}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Variabelen van eerder falende constraints zijn aangepast, constraints herevalueren}
\STATE $\mbox{ok}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$
\STATE $j\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf Backup}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$
\WHILE{$\mbox{ok}\wedge j<\mbox{depth}$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf Checkdepth}\left( \mbox{depth},k \right)}\leftarrow j$\COMMENT{Gecontroleerde diepte aanpassen}
\STATE $\mbox{ok}\leftarrow\mbox{ok}\wedge c\left(z_{j},z_{\mbox{depth}}\right)$
\STATE $j\leftarrow j+1$
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\mbox{ok}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{alle constraints zijn geaccepteerd}
\IF{$\mbox{depth}=N$}
\STATE\COMMENT{diepte bereikt, rapporteren}
\RETURN $z_1,z_2,\ldots,z_n$
\ELSE[Verder uitdiepen]
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf backmarking}\left( \mbox{depth}+1 \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\ENDIF
\FOR{$j=\mbox{depth}$\  to $N$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf Backup}\left( j \right)}\leftarrow\mbox{depth}-1$\COMMENT{Variabele aangepast (diepte naar omhoog)}
\ENDFOR
\ENDFOR
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7355}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7355
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Arc Consistency 3}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{Queue}\leftarrow\left\{c\left(z_i,z_j\right)|i<j\right\}$
\WHILE{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf notEmpty}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$}
\STATE$c\left(z_i,z_j\right)\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf dequeue}\left( \mbox{Queue} \right)}$
\STATE$d_{i}'\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf domain}\left( z_i \right)}$
\STATE$d_{j}'\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf domain}\left( z_j \right)}$
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf removeInconsistentValuesOf}\left( z_i,z_j,c\left(z_i,z_j\right) \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf domain}\left( z_i \right)}\neq d_i'$}
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueue}\left( \mbox{Queue},\left\{c\left(z_j,z_i\right)|\forall j:j<i\right\}\cup\left\{c\left(z_i,z_j\right)|\forall j:i<j\right\} \right)}$
\ENDIF
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf domain}\left( z_j \right)}\neq d_j'$}
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf enqueue}\left( \mbox{Queue},\left\{c\left(z_j,z_i\right)|\forall i:j<i\right\}\cup\left\{c\left(z_i,z_j\right)|\forall i:i<j\right\} \right)}$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24260}%
$ =0$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7447}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7447
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimax}\left( \mbox{board},\mbox{depth} \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\IF{$\mbox{depth}<\mbox{depthbound}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Einde nog niet bereikt}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf isMaxLevel}\left( \mbox{depth} \right)}$}
\STATE$M\leftarrow-\infty$
\FORALL{$c\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf children}\left( \mbox{board} \right)}$}
\STATE M=\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf max}_{}\left( M,\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimax}\left( c,\mbox{depth}+1 \right)} \right)}
\ENDFOR
\RETURN $M$
\ELSE
\STATE$m\leftarrow\infty$
\FORALL{$c\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf children}\left( \mbox{board} \right)}$}
\STATE m=\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf min}_{}\left( m,\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf minimax}\left( c,\mbox{depth}+1 \right)} \right)}
\ENDFOR
\RETURN $m$
\ENDIF
\ELSE
\STATE\COMMENT{Eind-diepte bereikt}
\RETURN $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf eval}\left( \mbox{board} \right)}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\foreach\x/\xxa/\yxa in {-3.5/0/2,1.5/1/2,5/1/1} {
  \draw (-0.5*0.87+4*\x,0.5*0.29+3) -- (0.5*0.87+4*\x,0.5*0.29+3);
  \draw (-0.5*0.87+4*\x,-0.5*0.29+3) -- (0.5*0.87+4*\x,-0.5*0.29+3);
  \draw (-0.5*0.29+4*\x,0.5*0.87+3) -- (-0.5*0.29+4*\x,-0.5*0.87+3);
  \draw (0.5*0.29+4*\x,-0.5*0.87+3) -- (0.5*0.29+4*\x,0.5*0.87+3);
  \draw[thick] (0.29*\xxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+3) -- (0.29*\xxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+3);
  \draw[thick] (0.29*\xxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+3) -- (0.29*\xxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+3);
}%(+\dx*\x,+\dy)
\foreach\x/\xxa/\yxa/\xoa/\yoa in {-5.5/0/2/0/1,-4.5/0/2/1/1,-3.5/0/2/0/0,-2.5/0/2/1/0,-1.5/0/2/2/0,-0.5/1/2/0/2,0.5/1/2/0/1,1.5/1/2/1/1,2.5/1/2/0/0,3.5/1/2/1/0,4.5/1/1/0/2,5.5/1/1/1/2} {
  \draw (-0.5*0.87+4*\x,0.5*0.29+2*3) -- (0.5*0.87+4*\x,0.5*0.29+2*3);
  \draw (-0.5*0.87+4*\x,-0.5*0.29+2*3) -- (0.5*0.87+4*\x,-0.5*0.29+2*3);
  \draw (-0.5*0.29+4*\x,0.5*0.87+2*3) -- (-0.5*0.29+4*\x,-0.5*0.87+2*3);
  \draw (0.5*0.29+4*\x,-0.5*0.87+2*3) -- (0.5*0.29+4*\x,0.5*0.87+2*3);
  \draw[thick] (0.29*\xxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29-0.5*0.125+2*3) -- (0.29*\xxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+4*\x,0.29*\yxa-0.29+0.5*0.125+2*3);

\stepcounter{subsection}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7509}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7509
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf taperingSearch}\left( \mbox{state},\mbox{depth},\mbox{depthbound} \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\IF{$\mbox{depth}<\mbox{depthbound}$}
\STATE\COMMENT{Einde nog niet bereikt}
\STATE $C\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf children}\left( \mbox{state} \right)}$
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf quickSort}\left( C,\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf eval}\left( C_i \right)} \right)}$
\FOR{$i=0$\  to $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf min}_{}\left( \#C,\mbox{depthbound} \right)}-1$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf taperingSearch}\left( R\left[i\right],\mbox{depth}+1,\mbox{depthbound}-1-i \right)}$
\ENDFOR
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\begin{displaymath}\begin{array}{rcll} T\vDash F&\Leftrightarrow&\forall m\in\ensuremath{\mbox{model}\left( T \right)}:T\displaystyle\rightarrow_mF&\mbox{\{Elk model $m$\  van $T$\  maakt $F$\  waar\}}\\&\Leftrightarrow&\forall m\in\ensuremath{\mbox{model}\left( T \right)}:\neg\left(T\displaystyle\rightarrow_m\neg F\right)&\mbox{\{Elk model $m$\  van $T$\  maakt $\neg F$\  onwaar\}}\\&\Leftrightarrow&\neg\exists m\in\ensuremath{\mbox{model}\left( T\cup\left\{\neg F\right\} \right)}&\mbox{\{Er bestaat geen model voor $T\cup\left\{\neg F\right\}$\}}\\&\Leftrightarrow&\ensuremath{\mbox{inconsistent}\left( T\cup\left\{\neg F\right\} \right)}&\mbox{\{$T\cup\left\{\neg F\right\}$\  is inconsistent\}} \end{array}\end{displaymath}%

\lthtmlinlinemathZ

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24613}%
\begin{displaymath}
% latex2html id marker 24613
\begin{array}{lr} &\textcolor{red}{B_1}\\&\textcolor{green}{B_2}\\&\vdots\\&\textcolor{blue}{B_n}\\\therefore&\textcolor{orange}{A}\leftarrow \textcolor{red}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{blue}{B_n}\\\hline &\textcolor{orange}{A} \end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7832}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7832
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Voorwaartse oplossingsstrategie voor gegronde horn clause}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\REQUIRE $F=C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m$
\STATE $\mbox{Derived}\leftarrow\varnothing$
\REPEAT
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectOne}\left( T,A\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n,A\notin\mbox{Derived}\wedge\forall i: B_i\in\mbox{Derived} \right)}$
\STATE$\mbox{Derived}\leftarrow\mbox{Derived}\cup\left\{A\right\}$
\UNTIL{$\forall i:C_i\in\mbox{Derived}\vee\neg \ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( T,A\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n,A\notin\mbox{Derived}\wedge\forall i: B_i\in\mbox{Derived} \right)}$}
\IF{$\forall i:C_i\in\mbox{Derived}$}
\RETURN $T\vDash F$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24633}%
$ \leftarrow F$%

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7893}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7893
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Achterwaardse oplossingsstrategie voor gegronde horn clause}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\REQUIRE $F=B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n$
\STATE $\mbox{goal}:=\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n$
\REPEAT
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectOne}\left( T,B_i\leftarrow C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m,B_i\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf body}\left( \mbox{goal} \right)} \right)}$
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf bodyReplace}\left( \mbox{goal},B_i,C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m \right)}$
\UNTIL{$\neg \ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( T,B_i\leftarrow C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m,B_i\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf body}\left( \mbox{goal} \right)} \right)}\vee\mbox{goal}=\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow$}
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage

\lthtmlinlinemathZ

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm7997}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 7997
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Achterwaardse oplossingsstrategie voor Horn Clause (met substitutie)}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\REQUIRE $F=B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n$
\STATE $\mbox{goal}:=\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n$
\REPEAT
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectOne}\left( T,B_i'\leftarrow C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m,\exists B_i\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf body}\left( \mbox{goal} \right)}\wedge\exists\theta=\ensuremath{\mbox{mgu}\left( B_i,B_i' \right)} \right)}$
\STATE$\mbox{goal}:=\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow\left(B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_{i-1}\wedge C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m\wedge B_{i-1}\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n\right)\cdot\theta$
\UNTIL{$\neg \ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( T,B_i'\leftarrow C_1\wedge C_2\wedge\ldots\wedge C_m,\exists B_i\in\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf body}\left( \mbox{goal} \right)}\wedge\exists\theta=\ensuremath{\mbox{mgu}\left( B_i,B_i' \right)} \right)}\vee\mbox{goal}=\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow$}
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24794}%
$ =\left\{A/B\right\}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8013}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8013
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Generatie van de Meest Algemene Unifier $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf mgu}\left( A,B \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mbox{mgu}\leftarrow\left\{A/B\right\}$
\STATE $\mbox{stop}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf false}$
\STATE $\mbox{error}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf false}$
\WHILE{$\neg\mbox{stop}\wedge\neg\mbox{error}$}
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\notin\mbox{variables}\wedge t\in\mbox{variables} \right)}$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\notin\mbox{variables}\wedge t\in\mbox{variables} \right)}$
\STATE $\mbox{mgu}\leftarrow\left(\mbox{mgu}\setminus\left\{s/t\right\}\right)\cup\left\{t/s\right\}$
\ELSIF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\in\mbox{variables}\wedge s=t \right)}$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\in\mbox{variables}\wedge s=t \right)}$
\STATE $\mbox{mgu}\leftarrow\mbox{mgu}\setminus\left\{s/t\right\}$
\ELSIF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\in\mbox{variables}\wedge t\notin\mbox{variables}\wedge s\in t \right)}$}
\STATE $\mbox{error}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$\COMMENT{$s$\  is een parameter in $t$}
\ELSIF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\in\mbox{variables}\wedge\exists u/v\in\mbox{mgu}\wedge s/t\neq u/v\wedge \left(s\in u\vee s\in v\right) \right)}$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s\in\mbox{variables}\wedge\exists u/v\in\mbox{mgu}\wedge s/t\neq u/v\wedge \left(s=u\vee s=v\right) \right)}$
\STATE $\theta\leftarrow\left\{s/t\right\}$
\FORALL{$u/v\in\mbox{mgu}$}
\IF{$s/t\neq u/v$}
\STATE $\mbox{mgu}\leftarrow\left(\mbox{mgu}\setminus\left\{u/v\right\}\right)\cup\left(\left\{u/v\right\}\cdot\theta\right)$\COMMENT{pas substitutie toe op alle elementen}
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\ELSIF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf selectionPossible}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s=f\left(s_1,s_2,\ldots s_n\right)\wedge t=g\left(t_1,t_2,\ldots t_m\right) \right)}$}
\STATE $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( \mbox{mgu},s/t,s=f\left(s_1,s_2,\ldots s_n\right)\wedge t=g\left(t_1,t_2,\ldots t_m\right) \right)}$
\IF{$f\neq g\vee m\neq n$}
\STATE $\mbox{error}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$\COMMENT{Verschillende functies of ander aantal parameters}
\ELSE
\STATE $\mbox{mgu}\leftarrow\left(\mbox{mgu}\setminus\left\{s/t\right\}\right)\cup\left\{s_1/t_1,s_2/t_2,\ldots,s_n/t_n\right\}$
\ENDIF
\ELSE
\STATE $\mbox{stop}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$\COMMENT{Niets meer aan te passen, algoritme is ten einde}
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\neg\mbox{error}$}
\RETURN $\mbox{mgu}$
\ELSE
\RETURN $\mbox{failure}$
\ENDIF
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24805}%
$ \forall x_1,\forall x_2\ldots,\forall x_k\  A_1\vee A_2\vee\ldots\vee A_m\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24807}%
\begin{displaymath}\begin{array}{c} \forall x_1,\forall x_2\ldots,\forall x_k\  A_1\vee A_2\vee\ldots\vee A_i\vee\ldots\vee A_m\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n\\\Updownarrow\\\forall x_1,\forall x_2\ldots,\forall x_k\  A_i\leftarrow B_1\wedge B_2\wedge\ldots\wedge B_n\wedge\neg A_1\wedge\neg A_2\wedge\ldots\neg A_{i-1}\wedge\neg A_{i+1}\wedge\ldots\wedge A_m \end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24809}%
\begin{displaymath}
% latex2html id marker 24809
\begin{array}{lr} &\textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{red}{A_m}\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{blue}{B_i}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n}\\\therefore&\textcolor{orange}{C_1}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_j}\vee\textcolor{cyan}{B_i'}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_{j+1}}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_k}\leftarrow\textcolor{brown}{D_1}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge\textcolor{brown}{D_l}\\\hline &\left(\textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{red}{A_m}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_1}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_j}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_{j+1}}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_k}\right.\\&\left.\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_{i-1}}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_1}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_m}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_{i+1}}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n}\right)\cdot\textcolor{purple}{\theta}\\\multicolumn{2}{c}{\textcolor{purple}{\theta}=\ensuremath{\mbox{mgu}\left( \textcolor{blue}{B_i},\textcolor{cyan}{B_i'} \right)}} \end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

$\displaystyle \left\{\begin{array}{c} \textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\textcolor{red}{A_m}\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{blue}{B_i}\wedge\ldots\wedge\textcolor{cyan}{B_i'}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n}\\\textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{blue}{A_i}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{cyan}{A_i'}\vee\ldots\textcolor{red}{A_m}\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n} \end{array}\right.$%

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath24820}%
\begin{displaymath}
% latex2html id marker 24820
\begin{array}{lr|l} &\textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\textcolor{red}{A_m}\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{blue}{B_i}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n}&N=m+n\\\therefore&\textcolor{orange}{C_1}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_j}\vee\textcolor{cyan}{B_i'}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_{j+1}}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_k}\leftarrow\textcolor{brown}{D_1}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge\textcolor{brown}{D_l}&M=k+l+1\\\hline &\left(\textcolor{red}{A_1}\vee\textcolor{red}{A_2}\vee\ldots\textcolor{red}{A_m}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_1}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_2}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_j}\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_{j+1}}\vee\ldots\vee\textcolor{orange}{C_k}\right.\\&\left.\leftarrow \textcolor{green}{B_1}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_{i-1}}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_1}\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_2}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{brown}{D_m}\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_{i+1}}\wedge\ldots\wedge \textcolor{green}{B_n}\right)\cdot\textcolor{purple}{\theta}&N+M-2\\\multicolumn{2}{c}{\textcolor{purple}{\theta}=\ensuremath{\mbox{mgu}\left( \textcolor{blue}{B_i},\textcolor{cyan}{B_i'} \right)}} \end{array}\end{displaymath}%

\stepcounter{paragraph}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline24838}%
$ S=T\cup\left\{\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow F\right\}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8344}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8344
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Generatie van de Meest Algemene Unifier $\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf mgu}\left( A,B \right)}$}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\REQUIRE$S$\COMMENT{Theorie op inconsistentie te bewijzen}
\STATE $\mbox{consistent}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf false}$
\STATE $\mbox{inconsistent}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf false}$
\WHILE{$\neg\mbox{consistent}\wedge\neg\mbox{inconsistent}$}
\IF{$\left(\mbox{\bf false}\leftarrow\right)\in S$}
\STATE$\mbox{inconsistent}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$
\ELSIF{$\exists G,H\in S:\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf resolvable}\left( G,H \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf resolved}\left( G,H \right)}$}
\STATE$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf select}\left( S,\left(G,H\right),G,H\in S:\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf resolvable}\left( G,H \right)}\wedge\neg\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf resolved}\left( G,H \right)} \right)}$
\STATE$I\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf factor}\left( \ensuremath{\mbox{\bf resolvent}\left( G,H \right)} \right)}$
\STATE$S\leftarrow S\cup\left\{I\right\}$
\ELSE
\STATE$\mbox{consistent}\leftarrow\mbox{\bf true}$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8557}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8557
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Simulated Annealing}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $S\leftarrow S_{\mbox{start}}$\COMMENT{$S$\  is de huidige oplossings-staat}
\STATE $c\leftarrow c_i$\COMMENT{zet de controle parameter op een initiele waarde}
\STATE $L\leftarrow L_i$\COMMENT{initi\"ele herhalingslengte}
\WHILE{$c>c_f$}
\FOR{$l=1$\  to $L$}
\STATE $S_j\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf generateNextRandomStep}\left( S \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf random}\left( 0,1 \right)}<e^{f\left(S_j\right)-f\left(S\right)/c}$}
\STATE $S\leftarrow S_j$
\ENDIF
\ENDFOR
\STATE $c\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf changeControl}\left( c \right)}$
\STATE $L\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf changeLength}\left( L \right)}$
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
\stepcounter{subsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8583}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8583
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Variable Neighbourhood Search}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mathfrak{H}\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Set van neighbourhood structuren}
\STATE $x\leftarrow x_0$\COMMENT{Initiele oplossing}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\WHILE{$l<\#\mathfrak{H}$}
\STATE $x'\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf bestNeighbourByStructure}\left( x,\mathfrak{H}\left[l\right] \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x' \right)}>\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x \right)}$}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $x\leftarrow x'$
\ELSE
\STATE $l\leftarrow l+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8605}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8605
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Variable Neighbourhood Search Reduced}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mathfrak{H}\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Set van neighbourhood structuren}
\STATE $x\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Initiele oplossing}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\WHILE{$l<\#\mathfrak{H}$}
\STATE $x'\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf randomNeighbourByStructure}\left( x,\mathfrak{H}\left[l\right] \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x' \right)}>\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x \right)}$}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $x\leftarrow x'$
\ELSE
\STATE $l\leftarrow l+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8624}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8624
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Variable Neighbourhood Search Basic}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mathfrak{H}\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Set van neighbourhood structuren}
\STATE $x\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Initiele oplossing}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\WHILE{$l<\#\mathfrak{H}$}
\STATE $x'\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf randomNeighbourByStructure}\left( x,\mathfrak{H}\left[l\right] \right)}$
\STATE $x''\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf bestNeighbourByStructure}\left( x',\mathfrak{H}\left[l\right] \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x'' \right)}>\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x \right)}$}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $x\leftarrow x''$
\ELSE
\STATE $l\leftarrow l+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\stepcounter{subsubsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline25167}%
$ k_{\mbox{max}}$%
\lthtmlinlinemathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{algorithm8648}%
\begin{algorithm}
% latex2html id marker 8648
[htb]                      % enter the algorithm environment
\caption{Variable Neighbourhood Search General}          % give the algorithm a caption
% and a label for \ref{} commands later in the document
\begin{algorithmic}[1]                    % enter the algorithmic environment
\STATE $\mathfrak{H}\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Set van neighbourhood structuren}
\STATE $x\leftarrow$\COMMENT{Initiele oplossing}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $k\leftarrow 0$
\WHILE{$k<k_{\mbox{max}}$}
\STATE $x'\leftarrow x$
\WHILE{$l<\#\mathfrak{H}$}
\STATE $x''\leftarrow\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf bestNeighbourByStructure}\left( x',\mathfrak{H}\left[l\right] \right)}$
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x'' \right)}>\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x' \right)}$}
\STATE $l\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $x'\leftarrow x''$
\ELSE
\STATE $l\leftarrow l+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\IF{$\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x' \right)}>\ensuremath{\mbox{\bf utility}\left( x \right)}$}
\STATE $k\leftarrow 0$
\STATE $x\leftarrow x'$
\ELSE
\STATE $k\leftarrow k+1$
\ENDIF
\ENDWHILE
\end{algorithmic}
\end{algorithm}%
\lthtmlfigureZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\begin{tikzpicture}[algor/.style={draw=green,thick,fill=green!50,font=\itshape },principle/.style={shape=rectangle,rounded corners=2mm,draw=blue,thick,fill=blue!50},hasinspired/.style={thick,->},hasinspirednoarrow/.style={thick},withprinciple/.style={thick,}]
\fill[red!35] (-2,-0.5) rectangle (15,4.5);

\node[algor] (smbas) at (12,15) {Simplified Memory-Bounded A*};

\stepcounter{subsection}
{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlfigureA{figure8807}%
\begin{figure}\centering
\begin{tikzpicture}[taal/.style={anchor=north west,text width=90pt},conceptgroup/.style={draw=blue,fill=blue!50, rounded corners=2mm, thick,minimum width=60mm,minimum height=20mm},hasinfluence/.style={blue,thick,->},algor/.style={draw=green,thick,fill=green!50,font=\itshape },algorinfluence/.style={green,thick,->}]
